When she learned that we were here for tourism, she sent me a travel guide to Wuxi and recommendations for popular restaurants, which was really useful for us who came to Wuxi for the first time.

Facilities: The hotel is in a good location, next to the stadium, and convenient for subway travel. There is also a MixC shopping mall next to it, which is very convenient for shopping and eating. The hotel facilities are also very complete, especially the sound of the TV can be projected into the bathroom, and you can watch movies immersively while taking a bath, and it is also a three-dimensional surround sound, which is great. The hotel's swimming pool is also very nice, the water is very clean, and for swimming enthusiasts, it is great to go swimming at any time during your stay. The hotel's breakfast is varied and delicious, especially pancakes and sesame paste, which is rare in other hotel breakfasts. There is also coffee for breakfast in the hotel, which is not only delicious, but also very user-friendly. There are two coffee machines in the restaurant, one for guests eating in the store, and the other is placed near the door of the restaurant, so that guests can pack a cup of coffee to take away after eating. For a heavy coffee lover, this is undoubtedly too heartwarming!

Hygiene: When traveling with children, the hotel must be clean and hygienic. The hygiene of this hotel has always been very good, and it is very reassuring to stay.

Service: The overall staff of the hotel are great, warm reception, and answer various questions and provide help, making people feel at home, very warm. Rita is very attentive. After seeing us check in, she took the initiative to ask if there are any items in the room that need to be replenished, and took the initiative to send us a few bottles of water. I have to say that such thoughtful service is very touching. It makes people feel at home while traveling.

This stay experience is perfect. When I come to Wuxi in the future, I will still stay in Crown. I would like to thank all the staff of the hotel.
